MORA (SUN) 01/01/1984 Toreo de Cuatro Caminos, Naucalpan, Estado de México [SL470]

## second defense for Hamada

## Dos won the right to face Enrique Vera. Dos won in straight falls.
6) el Signo COR Villano III [UWA JLH]
## third defense for Signo. Bloody match. Signo knock Villano into the seats, Villano was stuck and could not return.
